        const searchForm = document.getElementById(&quot;search-form&quot;);
        const searchBox = document.getElementById(&quot;search-box&quot;);
        const resultsContainer = document.getElementById(&quot;results-container&quot;);
        const resultsDiv = document.getElementById(&quot;results&quot;);
        const noResultsMessage = document.getElementById(&quot;no-results&quot;);
        const loadingIndicator = document.querySelector(&quot;.loading-indicator&quot;);

        searchForm.addEventListener(&quot;submit&quot;, (event) =&gt; {
            event.preventDefault();
            const searchTerm = searchBox.value.trim();

            if (searchTerm === &quot;&quot;) {
                alert(&quot;検索キーワードを入力してください。&quot;);
                return;
            }

            resultsContainer.style.display = &quot;none&quot;;
            noResultsMessage.style.display = &quot;none&quot;;
            resultsDiv.innerHTML = &quot;&quot;;
            loadingIndicator.style.display = &quot;block&quot;;

            // ここにGoogle Apps ScriptのURLを記述します
            const scriptUrl = &quot;https://script.google.com/a/macros/xn--cjrvv93jfsd7qwrlf746asjosvy.net/s/AKfycbxoTJtlL0MadaorrHiQTEg5Rrujj8kB-Csn_2O0FKfR8z40yC6I8vS5pBOX1S_EMJ6DHA/exec&quot;; // 例：https://script.google.com/macros/xxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx/exec

            fetch(scriptUrl + &quot;?action=search&amp;searchTerm=&quot; + encodeURIComponent(searchTerm))
                .then((response) =&gt; response.json())
                .then((data) =&gt; {
                    loadingIndicator.style.display = &quot;none&quot;;
                    if (data.length &gt; 0) {
                        displayResults(data);
                        resultsContainer.style.display = &quot;block&quot;;
                    } else {
                        noResultsMessage.style.display = &quot;block&quot;;
                    }
                })
                .catch((error) =&gt; {
                    loadingIndicator.style.display = &quot;none&quot;;
                    alert(&quot;検索中にエラーが発生しました: &quot; + error.message);
                    console.error(&quot;Error:&quot;, error);
                });
        });

        function displayResults(results) {
            resultsDiv.innerHTML = &quot;&quot;;
            results.forEach(row =&gt; {
                for (const key in row) {
                    if (row.hasOwnProperty(key)) {
                        const resultItem = document.createElement(&quot;div&quot;);
                        resultItem.classList.add(&quot;result-item&quot;);

                        const label = document.createElement(&quot;div&quot;);
                        label.classList.add(&quot;result-label&quot;);
                        label.textContent = key;

                        const value = document.createElement(&quot;div&quot;);
                        value.classList.add(&quot;result-value&quot;);

                        if (key === &quot;投与速度、投与上限&quot; || key === &quot;その他注意事項&quot;) {
                            // 通常の改行は&lt;br&gt;に置換
                            const formattedValue = row[key].replace(/\n/g, &#39;&lt;br&gt;&#39;);
                            value.innerHTML = formattedValue;
                        } else if ((key === &quot;溶解・調製時の注意および配合変化&quot;) &amp;&amp; typeof row[key] === &#39;string&#39;) {
                            const formattedValue = row[key].replace(/\n/g, &#39;&lt;br&gt;&#39;);
                            value.innerHTML = formattedValue;
                        }
                         else {
                            value.textContent = row[key];
                        }

                        resultItem.appendChild(label);
                        resultItem.appendChild(value);
                        resultsDiv.appendChild(resultItem);
                    }
                }
                // 各薬剤情報の間に区切り線を追加する場合
                if (results.indexOf(row) &lt; results.length - 1) {
                    const separator = document.createElement(&quot;hr&quot;);
                    resultsDiv.appendChild(separator);
                }
            });
        }

font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; vertical-align: baseline;">配合変化とは、2種類以上の注射薬を混合することで生じる物理的化学的反応です。注射薬は、単独で安定性が維持できるように製剤設計されているため、混合すると着色、混濁、沈殿、結晶析出といった外観変化や含量低下などが生じる場合があります。</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #222222; font-family: Verdana, Arial; font-size: 10.5pt; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">含量が低下すると、期待している注射薬の効果を十分に発揮できなくなり患者に不利益をもたらします。</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #222222; font-family: Verdana, Arial; font-size: 10.5pt; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; vertical-align: baseline;">また、フィルタやルート閉塞が起こり、医療器具が使用不可能になることもあります。</span></p><p  dir="ltr" class="zfr3Q CDt4Ke " style="background-color: transparent; border-bottom: none; border-left: none; border-right: none; border-top: none; line-height: 2.057148; margin-bottom: 21.0pt; margin-top: 12.0pt; padding-bottom: 0.0pt; padding-left: 0.0pt; padding-right: 0.0pt; padding-top: 0.0pt;"><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #222222; font-family: Verdana, Arial; font-size: 10.5pt; font-weight: 400; vertical-align: baseline;">　</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #222222; font-family: Verdana, Arial; font-size: 10.5pt; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; vertical-align: baseline;">そこで、「配合変化が起き得る組み合わせを覚えておけば対応できるのでは？」と考える方もいるでしょう。しかし、その組み合わせは膨大であり、全てを覚えておくことは現実的ではありません。そこで</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #222222; font-family: Verdana, Arial; font-size: 10.5pt; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">添付文書、インタビューフォーム内容を基に</span><span class="C9DxTc " style="color: #222222; font-family: Verdana, Arial; font-size: 10.5pt; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; vertical-align: baseline;">確認ができるツールを用意しました。</span></p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></section><section         const searchForm = document.getElementById(&quot;search-form&quot;);
        const searchBox = document.getElementById(&quot;search-box&quot;);
        const resultsContainer = document.getElementById(&quot;results-container&quot;);
        const resultsDiv = document.getElementById(&quot;results&quot;);
        const noResultsMessage = document.getElementById(&quot;no-results&quot;);
        const loadingIndicator = document.querySelector(&quot;.loading-indicator&quot;);

        searchForm.addEventListener(&quot;submit&quot;, (event) =&gt; {
            event.preventDefault();
            const searchTerm = searchBox.value.trim();

            if (searchTerm === &quot;&quot;) {
                alert(&quot;検索キーワードを入力してください。&quot;);
                return;
            }

            resultsContainer.style.display = &quot;none&quot;;
            noResultsMessage.style.display = &quot;none&quot;;
            resultsDiv.innerHTML = &quot;&quot;;
            loadingIndicator.style.display = &quot;block&quot;;

            // ここにGoogle Apps ScriptのURLを記述します
            const scriptUrl = &quot;https://script.google.com/a/macros/xn--cjrvv93jfsd7qwrlf746asjosvy.net/s/AKfycbxoTJtlL0MadaorrHiQTEg5Rrujj8kB-Csn_2O0FKfR8z40yC6I8vS5pBOX1S_EMJ6DHA/exec&quot;; // 例：https://script.google.com/macros/xxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx/exec

            fetch(scriptUrl + &quot;?action=search&amp;searchTerm=&quot; + encodeURIComponent(searchTerm))
                .then((response) =&gt; response.json())
                .then((data) =&gt; {
                    loadingIndicator.style.display = &quot;none&quot;;
                    if (data.length &gt; 0) {
                        displayResults(data);
                        resultsContainer.style.display = &quot;block&quot;;
                    } else {
                        noResultsMessage.style.display = &quot;block&quot;;
                    }
                })
                .catch((error) =&gt; {
                    loadingIndicator.style.display = &quot;none&quot;;
                    alert(&quot;検索中にエラーが発生しました: &quot; + error.message);
                    console.error(&quot;Error:&quot;, error);
                });
        });

        function displayResults(results) {
            resultsDiv.innerHTML = &quot;&quot;;
            results.forEach(row =&gt; {
                for (const key in row) {
                    if (row.hasOwnProperty(key)) {
                        const resultItem = document.createElement(&quot;div&quot;);
                        resultItem.classList.add(&quot;result-item&quot;);

                        const label = document.createElement(&quot;div&quot;);
                        label.classList.add(&quot;result-label&quot;);
                        label.textContent = key;

                        const value = document.createElement(&quot;div&quot;);
                        value.classList.add(&quot;result-value&quot;);

                        if (key === &quot;投与速度、投与上限&quot; || key === &quot;その他注意事項&quot;) {
                            // 通常の改行は&lt;br&gt;に置換
                            const formattedValue = row[key].replace(/\n/g, &#39;&lt;br&gt;&#39;);
                            value.innerHTML = formattedValue;
                        } else if ((key === &quot;溶解・調製時の注意および配合変化&quot;) &amp;&amp; typeof row[key] === &#39;string&#39;) {
                            const formattedValue = row[key].replace(/\n/g, &#39;&lt;br&gt;&#39;);
                            value.innerHTML = formattedValue;
                        }
                         else {
                            value.textContent = row[key];
                        }

                        resultItem.appendChild(label);
                        resultItem.appendChild(value);
                        resultsDiv.appendChild(resultItem);
                    }
                }
                // 各薬剤情報の間に区切り線を追加する場合
                if (results.indexOf(row) &lt; results.length - 1) {
                    const separator = document.createElement(&quot;hr&quot;);
                    resultsDiv.appendChild(separator);
                }
            });
        }

        const searchBox = document.getElementById(&quot;search-box&quot;);
        const resultsContainer = document.getElementById(&quot;results-container&quot;);
        const resultsDiv = document.getElementById(&quot;results&quot;);
        const noResultsMessage = document.getElementById(&quot;no-results&quot;);
        const loadingIndicator = document.querySelector(&quot;.loading-indicator&quot;);

        searchForm.addEventListener(&quot;submit&quot;, (event) =&gt; {
            event.preventDefault();
            const searchTerm = searchBox.value.trim();

            if (searchTerm === &quot;&quot;) {
                alert(&quot;検索キーワードを入力してください。&quot;);
                return;
            }

            resultsContainer.style.display = &quot;none&quot;;
            noResultsMessage.style.display = &quot;none&quot;;
            resultsDiv.innerHTML = &quot;&quot;;
            loadingIndicator.style.display = &quot;block&quot;;

            // ここにGoogle Apps ScriptのURLを記述します
            const scriptUrl = &quot;https://script.google.com/a/macros/xn--cjrvv93jfsd7qwrlf746asjosvy.net/s/AKfycbxoTJtlL0MadaorrHiQTEg5Rrujj8kB-Csn_2O0FKfR8z40yC6I8vS5pBOX1S_EMJ6DHA/exec&quot;; // 例：https://script.google.com/macros/xxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx/exec

            fetch(scriptUrl + &quot;?action=search&amp;searchTerm=&quot; + encodeURIComponent(searchTerm))
                .then((response) =&gt; response.json())
                .then((data) =&gt; {
                    loadingIndicator.style.display = &quot;none&quot;;
                    if (data.length &gt; 0) {
                        displayResults(data);
                        resultsContainer.style.display = &quot;block&quot;;
                    } else {
                        noResultsMessage.style.display = &quot;block&quot;;
                    }
                })
                .catch((error) =&gt; {
                    loadingIndicator.style.display = &quot;none&quot;;
                    alert(&quot;検索中にエラーが発生しました: &quot; + error.message);
                    console.error(&quot;Error:&quot;, error);
                });
        });

        function displayResults(results) {
